        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: decimal;">
       <div class="mw-references-wrap mw-references-columns">
        <ol class="references">
         <li id="cite_note-1">
          <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
           <b>
            <a href="#cite_ref-1">
             ^
            </a>
           </b>
          </span>
          <span class="reference-text">
           Approximately 90% on standard
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Swadesh_lists" title="Swadesh lists">
            Swadesh lists
           </a>
           .
          </span>
         </li>
         <li id="cite_note-2">
          <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
           <b>
            <a href="#cite_ref-2">
             ^
            </a>
           </b>
          </span>
          <span class="reference-text">
           <a class="external free" href="http://etimologias.dechile.net/?riesgo" rel="nofollow">
            http://etimologias.dechile.net/?riesgo
           </a>
          </span>
         </li>
         <li id="cite_note-3">
          <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
           <b>
            <a href="#cite_ref-3">
             ^
            </a>
           </b>
          </span>
          <span class="reference-text">
           Curiously, the Portuguese term is the origin of both the Spanish and, via French, the English term, according to
           <a href="/wiki/Encarta#Encarta_Dictionary" title="Encarta">
            Microsoft Encarta Dictionary
           </a>
           , 2004. It is formed of
           <i>
            em
           </i>
           ('in', as a
           <a href="/wiki/Prefix" title="Prefix">
            prefix
           </a>
           ),
           <i>
            baraço
           </i>
           (an old term for 'rope') and
           <a href="/wiki/Suffix" title="Suffix">
            suffix
           </a>
           <i>
            -ada
           </i>
           (which is the feminine form of a verbal ending equivalent to "-ed"), according to its entry in
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dicion%C3%A1rio_Houaiss_da_L%C3%ADngua_Portuguesa" title="Dicionário Houaiss da Língua Portuguesa">
            Houaiss Dictionary
           </a>
           .
          </span>
         </li>
         <li id="cite_note-4">
          <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
           <b>
            <a href="#cite_ref-4">
             ^
            </a>
           </b>
          </span>
          <span class="reference-text">
           Martínez 2010, p. 135; Veciana 2004, p. 15
          </span>

         <li id="cite_note-61">
          <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
           <b>
            <a href="#cite_ref-61">
             ^
            </a>
           </b>
          </span>
          <span class="reference-text">
           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Novo_Dicion%C3%A1rio_da_L%C3%ADngua_Portuguesa" title="Novo Dicionário da Língua Portuguesa">
            Aurélio
           </a>
           defines the words
           <i>
            pra¹
           </i>
           as a syncopated form of
           <i>
            para
           </i>
           , and
           <i>
            pra²
           </i>
           and
           <i>
            pro
           </i>
           as a contraction of
           <i>
            pra¹
           </i>
           plus the article.
          </span>
         </li>
         <li id="cite_note-62">
          <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
           <b>
            <a href="#cite_ref-62">
             ^
            </a>
           </b>
          </span>
          <span class="reference-text">
           The phoneme represented by ⟨ll⟩ has merged with the one represented by ⟨y⟩ in most dialects, commonly realized as
           <span class="IPA" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)">
            [ʝ]
           </span>
           , or, in
           <a href="/wiki/Rioplatense_Spanish" title="Rioplatense Spanish">
            River Plate Spanish
           </a>
           , as
           <span class="IPA" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)">
            [ʒ]
           </span>
           or as
           <span class="IPA" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)">
            [ʃ]
           </span>
           .
          </span>
         </li>
         <li id="cite_note-63">
          <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
           <b>
            <a href="#cite_ref-63">
             ^
            </a>
           </b>
          </span>
          <span class="reference-text">
           <a class="external free" href="https://books.google.co.uk/books?id=XmB-BgAAQBAJ&amp;pg=PA54&amp;lpg=PA54&amp;dq=portuguese+celtic+phonology&amp;source=bl&amp;ots=TI6_dp08cM&amp;sig=HJRg557aN9rgD6VdE4np07diDNc&amp;hl=en&amp;sa=X&amp;ved=0ahUKEwidlaS4ofXUAhWsKcAKHbxSCrM4ChDoAQgqMAE#v=onepage&amp;q=portuguese%20celtic%20phonology&amp;f=false" rel="nofollow">
            https://books.google.co.uk/books?id=XmB-BgAAQBAJ&amp;pg=PA54&amp;lpg=PA54&amp;dq=portuguese+celtic+phonology&amp;source=bl&amp;ots=TI6_dp08cM&amp;sig=HJRg557aN9rgD6VdE4np07diDNc&amp;hl=en&amp;sa=X&amp;ved=0ahUKEwidlaS4ofXUAhWsKcAKHbxSCrM4ChDoAQgqMAE#v=onepage&amp;q=portuguese%20celtic%20phonology&amp;f=false
           </a>
          </span>
         </li>
         <li id="cite_note-64">
          <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
           <b>
            <a href="#cite_ref-64">
             ^
            </a>
           </b>
          </span>
          <span class="reference-text">
           <a class="external free" href="https://books.google.co.uk/books?id=FtxywY_6g4UC&amp;pg=PA29&amp;lpg=PA29&amp;dq=nasal+portuguese+celtic&amp;source=bl&amp;ots=rnPk6q2_pK&amp;sig=got6sv4vtMj0YVD7BagpBDC8O54&amp;hl=en&amp;sa=X&amp;ved=0ahUKEwjlws3zpPXUAhVGCMAKHR8OB4AQ6AEIRTAD#v=onepage&amp;q=nasal%20portuguese%20celtic&amp;f=false" rel="nofollow">
            https://books.google.co.uk/books?id=FtxywY_6g4UC&amp;pg=PA29&amp;lpg=PA29&amp;dq=nasal+portuguese+celtic&amp;source=bl&amp;ots=rnPk6q2_pK&amp;sig=got6sv4vtMj0YVD7BagpBDC8O54&amp;hl=en&amp;sa=X&amp;ved=0ahUKEwjlws3zpPXUAhVGCMAKHR8OB4AQ6AEIRTAD#v=onepage&amp;q=nasal%20portuguese%20celtic&amp;f=false
           </a>
          </span>
         </li>
        </ol>
       </div>
